                             # Evaluation Report                                                                                                                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Summary                                                                                                                                                                          
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             A libFuzzer run on Wiresharks AIM protocol dissector (`handler_aim`) triggered a buffer overflow detected by AddressSanitizer. The overflow occurs in the function                 
                             `aim_get_buddyname` (packet-aim.c:591) during a `memcpy` operation, leading to an abort via `__fortify_fail`.                                                                       
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Description                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             - Issue Nature                                                                                                                                                                      
                               During fuzz testing in interactive mode with libFuzzer, a malformed input caused AddressSanitizer to detect a buffer overflow in Wiresharks AIM dissector. The                   
                             crash is surfaced as an abort signal (`ABRT`) originating from fortified `memcpy`.                                                                                                  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             - Vulnerability Type                                                                                                                                                                
                               Buffer overflow in the AIM dissector code. The runtime check in `memcpy` via glibcs fortify mechanism (`__fortify_fail`) confirms the overflow condition.                        
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             - Key Observations                                                                                                                                                                  
                                The failure trace shows the abort is triggered by `raise()`  `abort()`  `__fortify_fail()`  `__chk_fail()`, indicating a built-in safety check caught an                     
                             out-of-bounds memory copy.                                                                                                                                                          
                                The faulty `memcpy` occurs in `aim_get_buddyname` (packet-aim.c:591).                                                                                                           
                                Call chain:                                                                                                                                                                     
                                  `aim_get_buddyname`                                                                                                                                                           
                                  `dissect_aim_chat_outgoing_msg` (packet-aim.c:1976)                                                                                                                           
                                  `dissect_aim_snac` (packet-aim.c:809)                                                                                                                                         
                                  `dissect_aim_pdu` (packet-aim.c:1618)                                                                                                                                         
                                  `tcp_dissect_pdus` (packet-tcp.c:5569)                                                                                                                                        
                                  Core dissector dispatch routines  `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`.                                                                                                                  
                                Fuzzing parameters included `-runs=100`, `-max_len=1024`, and AddressSanitizer instrumentation.                                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             - Code Areas for Investigation                                                                                                                                                      
                               To fully assess the issues scope, review and audit:                                                                                                                              
                               1. `aim_get_buddyname` implementation in `epan/dissectors/packet-aim.c` around line 591.                                                                                          
                               2. Buffer length checks and data parsing in `dissect_aim_chat_outgoing_msg` (line 1976).                                                                                          
                               3. SNAC-level parsing logic in `dissect_aim_snac` (line 809).                                                                                                                     
                               4. PDU assembly in `dissect_aim_pdu` (line 1618).                                                                                                                                 
                               5. Downstream handling in TCP dissector (`epan/dissectors/packet-tcp.c`) and frame dissector (`packet-frame.c`).                                                                  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             These areas encompass the data flow from raw input through protocol layers to the vulnerable copy operation.

                             ===Analysis Report===                                                                                                                                                               
                             # Analysis Report                                                                                                                                                                   
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Relevant Code Snippets                                                                                                                                                           
                             <code_snippets>                                                                                                                                                                     
                             <code>                                                                                                                                                                              
                             epan/dissectors/packet-aim.c:586-594                                                                                                                                                
                             ```                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             586:    *name = wmem_alloc(pool, 256);                                                                                                                                              
                             587:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             588:    buddyname_length = tvb_get_ntohs(tvb, offset);                                                                                                                              
                             589:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             590:    if (pool)                                                                                                                                                                   
                             591:            memcpy(*name, tvb_get_ptr(tvb,offset,1), buddyname_length);                                                                                                         
                             592:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             593:    return buddyname_length;                                                                                                                                                    
                             594:}                                                                                                                                                                               
                             ```                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             </code>                                                                                                                                                                             
                             <code>                                                                                                                                                                              
                             epan/dissectors/packet-aim.c:1971-1979                                                                                                                                              
                             ```                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             1971:   uint8_t *buddyname;                                                                                                                                                         
                             1972:   unsigned char *msg;                                                                                                                                                         
                             1973:   int buddyname_length;                                                                                                                                                       
                             1974:                                                                                                                                                                               
                             1975:   msg=(unsigned char *)wmem_alloc(pinfo->pool, 1000);                                                                                                                         
                             1976:   buddyname_length = aim_get_buddyname( pinfo->pool, &buddyname, tvb, 30 );                                                                                                   
                             1977:                                                                                                                                                                               
                             1978:   /* channel message from client */                                                                                                                                           
                             1979:   aim_get_message( msg, tvb, 40 + buddyname_length, tvb_reported_length(tvb)                                                                                                  
                             ```                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             </code>                                                                                                                                                                             
                             </code_snippets>                                                                                                                                                                    
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Fix Strategy                                                                                                                                                                     
                             <fix_strategy>                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             1. Overview and Root Cause                                                                                                                                                          
                                The crash stems from an unchecked `memcpy` in `aim_get_buddyname` (packet-aim.c:591). The code allocates a fixed 256-byte buffer but reads an untrusted length                   
                             (`buddyname_length`) from the packet and then:                                                                                                                                      
                                a. Uses `tvb_get_ptr(tvb, offset, 1)` which only guarantees a single byte pointer.                                                                                               
                                b. Copies `buddyname_length` bytes without verifying it is  256 or that the buffer region is contiguous.                                                                        
                                This allows both a heap overflow (writing past the 256-byte allocation) and a read-out-of-bounds on the tvbuff.                                                                  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             2. Preserve Existing Logic                                                                                                                                                          
                                - We must continue to read a 16-bit length from the packet and slice out that many bytes for the buddy name.                                                                     
                                - The caller (`dissect_aim_chat_outgoing_msg`) relies on the returned `buddyname_length` to compute the start of the next field (`aim_get_message`).                             
                                - We will clamp/truncate only when the fuzzed length exceeds safe bounds, and return the _used_ length so downstream parsing stays in sync.                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             3. Patch Steps                                                                                                                                                                      
                                a. Define a maximum buddy-name length constant:                                                                                                                                  
                                   ```c                                                                                                                                                                          
                                   #define AIM_BUDDYNAME_MAXLEN 255                                                                                                                                              
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                b. Change `aim_get_buddyname(pool, name, tvb, offset)` as follows:                                                                                                               
                                   - Read the 16-bit length at `offset`.                                                                                                                                         
                                   - Clamp it to `AIM_BUDDYNAME_MAXLEN`.                                                                                                                                         
                                   - Ensure the tvbuff has at least `clamped_length` bytes starting at `(offset + 2)` (after the length field).                                                                  
                                   - Allocate a `(AIM_BUDDYNAME_MAXLEN + 1)` buffer to allow null termination.                                                                                                   
                                   - Use `tvb_get_ptr(tvb, offset + 2, clamped_length)` to get a pointer guaranteed for `clamped_length`.                                                                        
                                   - Copy only `clamped_length` bytes into the buffer.                                                                                                                           
                                   - Null-terminate the buffer.                                                                                                                                                  
                                   - Return the _clamped_ length to the caller.                                                                                                                                  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                                c. Adjust the buffer allocation accordingly (e.g., `wmem_alloc(pool, AIM_BUDDYNAME_MAXLEN + 1)`).                                                                                
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             4. Detailed Implementation Plan                                                                                                                                                     
                                In `epan/dissectors/packet-aim.c`, around lines 586594:                                                                                                                         
                                1. Insert:                                                                                                                                                                       
                                   ```c                                                                                                                                                                          
                                   #define AIM_BUDDYNAME_MAXLEN 255                                                                                                                                              
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                2. Replace the body of `aim_get_buddyname(...)` with:                                                                                                                            
                                   ```c                                                                                                                                                                          
                                   int                                                                                                                                                                           
                                   aim_get_buddyname(wmem_allocator_t *pool, gchar **name, tvbuff_t *tvb, gint offset)                                                                                           
                                   {                                                                                                                                                                             
                                       guint16 raw_len;                                                                                                                                                          
                                       gint   buddyname_length, copy_len;                                                                                                                                        
                                       const guint8 *src;                                                                                                                                                        
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                                       /* Read length field */                                                                                                                                                   
                                       raw_len = tvb_get_ntohs(tvb, offset);                                                                                                                                     
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                                       /* Clamp to safe maximum */                                                                                                                                               
                                       copy_len = raw_len > AIM_BUDDYNAME_MAXLEN ? AIM_BUDDYNAME_MAXLEN : raw_len;                                                                                               
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                                       /* Ensure the tvbuff has enough data for the buddyname */                                                                                                                 
                                       if (!tvb_bytes_exist(tvb, offset + 2, copy_len)) {                                                                                                                        
                                           /* Malformed: data ends early */                                                                                                                                      
                                           *name = wmem_strdup_printf(pool, "<truncated:%u>", raw_len);                                                                                                          
                                           return 0;                                                                                                                                                             
                                       }                                                                                                                                                                         
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                                       /* Allocate 1 extra byte for null-terminator */                                                                                                                           
                                       *name = wmem_alloc(pool, AIM_BUDDYNAME_MAXLEN + 1);                                                                                                                       
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                                       /* Copy from the packet at offset+2 */                                                                                                                                    
                                       src = tvb_get_ptr(tvb, offset + 2, copy_len);                                                                                                                             
                                       memcpy(*name, src, copy_len);                                                                                                                                             
                                       (*name)[copy_len] = '\0';                                                                                                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                                       /* Return the _actual_ length consumed */                                                                                                                                 
                                       return copy_len;                                                                                                                                                          
                                   }                                                                                                                                                                             
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                3. Verify all calls that use the returned length (e.g., in `dissect_aim_chat_outgoing_msg`) remain correct: since they index the next field by adding the                        
                             returned length, truncation merely shifts parsing to the truncated boundary.                                                                                                        
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             5. Justification                                                                                                                                                                    
                                - **Bounds Safety**: We clamp `raw_len` to 255 so writes stay within the allocated buffer.                                                                                      
                                - **Pointer Validity**: Using `tvb_get_ptr(tvb, offset+2, copy_len)` ensures the returned pointer is valid for the requested read length or triggers our                         
                             truncation path.                                                                                                                                                                    
                                - **Downstream Logic Preservation**: By returning the exact number of bytes we actually consumed, the existing code in `dissect_aim_chat_outgoing_msg` will                      
                             continue to compute offsets correctly, maintaining protocol semantics for well-formed packets.                                                                                      
                                - **Fuzzer Compatibility**: We do not alter the harness or fuzzing logic, nor do we modify any external libraries or tests. Malformed inputs will now be                         
                             gracefully truncated or cause early return without overflow, and the dissector will continue parsing or skip gracefully.                                                            
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             6. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations                                                                                                                                             
                                - **Buddyname Truncation**: Very long buddy names get truncated, which is acceptable given the historical 255-byte cap and prevents crashes.                                     
                                - **Parsing Skips**: In cases where the tvbuff does not contain the full declared length, we return length 0 and emit a placeholder name; subsequent parsing                     
                             uses offset+0, so it will attempt to parse at the same point and likely hit other length checks or gracefully bail.                                                                 
                                - **Interoperability**: For legitimate packets with names >255 bytes (unlikely in AIM specs), this change truncates them. However, current code would crash. A                   
                             255-byte cap is a reasonable safety boundary.                                                                                                                                       
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             7. Verification                                                                                                                                                                     
                                - Add unit tests feeding an oversized buddyname length to `aim_get_buddyname`, verifying no crash and correct truncation.                                                        
                                - Rerun fuzz targets to confirm no more AddressSanitizer overflows in this path.                                                                                                 
                                - Confirm existing dissector tests still pass.                                                                                                                                   
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             </fix_strategy>                                                                                                                                                                     
                             ===Evaluation End===

                             +                                                                                                                                                                                   
                             +    /* Read and clamp length field to buffer size (255) */                                                                                                                         
                             +    raw_len = tvb_get_ntohs(tvb, offset);                                                                                                                                          
                             +    copy_len = raw_len > 255 ? 255 : raw_len;                                                                                                                                      
                             +                                                                                                                                                                                   
                             +    /* Ensure the tvbuff has enough data after the 2-byte length */                                                                                                                
                             +    if (!tvb_bytes_exist(tvb, offset + 2, copy_len)) {                                                                                                                             
                             +        *name = wmem_strdup_printf(pool, "<truncated:%u>", raw_len);                                                                                                               
                             +        return 0;                                                                                                                                                                  
                             +    }                                                                                                                                                                              
                             +                                                                                                                                                                                   
                             +    /* Allocate 256 bytes: 255 for name + 1 for null terminator */                                                                                                                 
                             +    *name = wmem_alloc(pool, 256);                                                                                                                                                 
                             +                                                                                                                                                                                   
                             +    src = tvb_get_ptr(tvb, offset + 2, copy_len);                                                                                                                                  
                             +    memcpy(*name, src, copy_len);                                                                                                                                                  
                             +    (*name)[copy_len] = '\0';                                                                                                                                                      
                             +                                                                                                                                                                                   
                             +    return copy_len;                                                                                                                                                               
                              }

                             ===Evaluation Report===                                                                                                                                                             
                             # Evaluation Report                                                                                                                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Summary                                                                                                                                                                          
                             The fuzzing harness for Wiresharks AIM dissector (`handler_aim`) triggers an AddressSanitizer abort when processing a crafted packet: a fortified `memcpy` in                      
                             `aim_get_buddyname` overruns the destination buffer. A patch was proposed to clamp the length, check available data, zero-terminate the copied name, and handle                     
                             truncated names via a formatted string. When this patch was applied, the build failed with an unused variable buddyname_length error, halting compilation.                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Description                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Initial Issue                                                                                                                                                                       
                             - A libFuzzer run on the `handler_aim` binary crashes under ASan with *** buffer overflow detected *** and aborts in `memcpy`.                                                    
                             - The stack trace pins the overflow in `aim_get_buddyname` (packet-aim.c:591), called by downstream functions like `dissect_aim_chat_outgoing_msg` and                              
                             `dissect_aim_snac`.                                                                                                                                                                 
                             - The vulnerable code reads a length field from the packet (`tvb_get_ntohs(tvb, offset)`) into a 256-byte allocation, then unconditionally `memcpy`s that many                      
                             bytes (potentially >256) without checking bounds or packet length.                                                                                                                  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Patch Attempt                                                                                                                                                                       
                             - The patch rewrote `aim_get_buddyname` to:                                                                                                                                         
                               1. Read the raw 16-bit length into `raw_len`.                                                                                                                                     
                               2. Clamp it to at most 255 bytes (`copy_len`).                                                                                                                                    
                               3. Check `tvb_bytes_exist` for `copy_len` bytes beyond the 2-byte length field; if not present, allocate a formatted \<truncated:\> string and return 0.                       
                               4. Allocate a fixed 256-byte buffer, copy `copy_len` bytes, null-terminate, and return the actual copied length.                                                                  
                             - The diff replaced the original code block (lines ~583596) with the new logic, introducing three new local variables: `guint16 raw_len; gint copy_len; const                      
                             guint8 *src;`.                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Patch Result                                                                                                                                                                        
                             - During compilation, an unused variable warning was elevated to an error by `-Werror`. Specifically, the original `uint16_t buddyname_length;` declared on line                    
                             584 was no longer used anywhere, triggering unused variable buddyname_length.                                                                                                   
                             - The build stopped immediately due to this error, so none of the new logic was compiled or tested.                                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Areas for Further Investigation                                                                                                                                                     
                             - Clean up or remove the unused `buddyname_length` declaration in `aim_get_buddyname`.                                                                                              
                             - Confirm that the offset logic accounts for the 2-byte length field when calculating where to read the name data (`offset + 2` vs. the original `offset`).                         
                             - Review related packet-parsing functions in `packet-aim.c` (e.g., `dissect_aim_snac`, `dissect_aim_chat_outgoing_msg`) to ensure length fields are interpreted and                 
                             bounds-checked consistently.                                                                                                                                                        
                             - Search for other uses of fortified string or buffer functions in the AIM dissector that may suffer similar over-reads or buffer-overflow risks.
